============= AMBs ============


============= SPI / BIOS CNTL =============

BIOS_CNTL = 0x0000 (IO)

0x0000 = BIOSWE - write enable
0x0000 = BLE - lock enable
0x0000 = SPI Read configuration
0x0000 = TopSwapStatus
0x0000 = SMM Bios Write Protect Disable
0x0000 = reserved

============= SPI Bar ==============

0x07ff0500 = BFPR - BIOS Flash primary region
0x0000e008 = HSFSTS - Hardware Sequencing Flash Status
0x00003f04 = HSFCTL - Hardware Sequencing Flash Control
0x0058efc0 = FADDR - Flash Address
0x00000000 = Reserved
0x00000000 = FDATA0
0x00000a0b = FRACC - Flash Region Access Permissions
0x00000000 = Flash Region 0
0x07ff0500 = Flash Region 1
0x04ff0003 = Flash Region 2
0x00020001 = Flash Region 3
0x00000fff = Flash Region 4
0x9fff07d0 = FPR0 Flash Protected Range 0
0x00000000 = FPR0 Flash Protected Range 1
0x00000000 = FPR0 Flash Protected Range 2
0x00000000 = FPR0 Flash Protected Range 3
0x00000000 = FPR0 Flash Protected Range 4
0x00000000 = SSFSTS - Software Sequencing Flash Status
0x00005006 = PREOP - Prefix opcode Configuration
0x0000143b = OPTYPE - Opcode Type Configuration
0x052003020601209f = OPMENU - Opcode Menu Configuration
0x00000000 = BBAR - BIOS Base Address Configuration
0x00000004 = FDOC - Flash Descriptor Observability Control
0x00000000 = Reserved
0x00000007 = AFC - Additional Flash Control
0x00802005 = LVSCC - Host Lower Vendor Specific Component Capabilities
0x00002005 = UVSCC - Host Upper Vendor Specific Component Capabilities
0x00000000 = FPB - Flash Partition Boundary
